 The Supreme Court dispute seems to be dragging at the moment
 haalanki baar council ne apni taraf se ise jald khatm karne kii taiyaari kar lee he
 In the Bar Council meeting held on Saturday evening, a committee of 7 members has been formed to resolve the issues of rebel judges
 is cameti ke sadsy jajon se milakar hal nikaalane kii koshish karenge
 Bar Council of India (BCI) has formed a seven-member team to discuss the current crisis with all other judges of the Supreme Court, except the five senior-most judges
 BCI ke adhyaksh manan kumaar mishra ne kaha ki team anya nyaayadhishon kii raay legi, unhone kaha ki is tarah ke muddon ko saarvajanik nahin kiya janaa chahie
 At the same time, the BCI said that whatever the differences between judges regarding the allocation of rosters or cases, it should be resolved through internal arrangements without publicly expressing opinion
 aapako bataa den ki is vivaad par baar council ke sabhi sadasyon ne shanivaar shaam ko baithak kii
 It was decided in the meeting that the justice system will not be allowed to be traumatized in any way
 baar council ne is maamle main supreme court ke sabhi jajon se sahyog kii apil kii he

 is vivaad ko puri tarah se jald sulajhane kii koshish ho rahi he

 baar council kii baithak main centre sarkaar ke us faisle kii tarif bhi kii gai, jisamen sarkaar ne is maamle main dakhal na dene kii baat kahi thi
 According to sources, Chief Justice Deepak Mishra can meet the four judges on Sunday evening
 justise chelmeshwar ke offis ke sutron ke mutabik shuukravaar ko justise chelmeshwar ke saath press conference karne vaale baaki ke teen jaj dilli se baahar hai, aise main justise chelmeshwar sijeai se milane ko icchhuk nahin hai or ye mulaakaat kal shaam ko ho sakati he

 chif justise ke baad duusare sabase senior jaj justise chelmeshwar ne press conference main kaha ki kabhi-kabhi hota he ki desh main supreme court kii vyavastha bhi badalati he
 He said that the administration of the Supreme Court is not working properly, if this continues, the democratic situation will not be good
 unhone kaha ki hamane is mudde par chif justise se baat kii, lekin unhone hamaari baat nahin suni
 The four judges said that if we did not put these things in front of the country and we did not speak, then democracy would end
 hamane chif justise se aniyamittaaon par baat kii

 chif justise par desh ko faisla karnaa chahie, ham bas desh kaa karj adaa kar rahe hai

K
 ke venugopal ne kaha ki shanivaar ko supreme court ke jajon ke bich sari takaraar khatm ho jaaegi or saare maamle sulajhaa liye jaaenge
 a committee headed by retired Supreme Court Judge DP Wadhwa has recommended the government take over control of fair price shops to curb corruption in the public distribution system
 samiti ne garibi rekha se upar jivan yaapan karne waalon ke liye saarvajanik vitaran pranali ke tahat sabsidi par khaadya saamagree dene kii vyavastha khatm karne kii bhi sifarish kii he
 In its final report submitted to the Supreme Court, the Justice Wadhwa Committee, while referring to the nexus between the owners, transporters, bureaucrats and leaders of fair price shops, said that it can be curbed only by implementing its recommendations
 samiti ne kaha he ki uchit dar dukaan hi bhrashtachar kaa kendra bindu he jahaan janata ko thagne ke liai iske maalik, transporter, naukarshah or netaaon main santh-ganth he
 According to the committee, real people are deprived of its benefits due to black marketing of food grains in the public distribution system
 aisi sthiti main behatar hoga ki bhrasht uchit dar dukaanon kaa sanchaalan sarkaar apane haath main le le
 For this it is necessary that a Civil Supplies Corporation should be formed in the states, which works independently under the public distribution system at the fair price shops to distribute food grains at the level of the fair price shops
 vadhwa samiti ne apni siforeeshon main kaha he ki uchit dar kii dukaane nijee vyaktiyon dwaara sanchalit karne kii bajaay behatar hoga yadi rajya str par nigam, panchayat raaj sansthaaen, sahakaari samitiyaan or mahilaon ke swa-sanchalit samooh inkaa sanchaalan karen
 The committee has said, "there should be a provision in the government budget to compensate for any loss in the operation of the corporation
" jahaan par uchit dar dukaanon ke liye dukaan or godaam nahin hai vahaan sarkaar or nigam ko madar deyari yaa atm yaa daakghar kii tarj par inkaa nirmaan karnaa chahie
 The command of such a corporation should be given to an officer of the Indian Administrative Service
 ’’ The Wadhwa Committee said that the category of families living above the poverty line should be abolished as it is a major means of sending food grains to the black market
 samiti ne kaha he ki yadi nyaayalay mahasoos karata he ki is shrenee ko khatm karnaa sambhav nahin he to is varg kaa dayera ek lakh rupye kii salanaa aamadani vaale pariwaron tak simit karne par vichaar kiya ja saktaa he
 According to the committee, everyone from the Prime Minister to the lower level has advocated to repair and reorganize the public distribution system
 is pranali ke punaruddhar ke liye kathor kadam uthaane kii aavashyaktaa he
 The comments report main kaha gaya he ki desh main paanch lakh se adhik uchit dar dukaanon se saarvajanik vitaran pranali ke tahat khadyann vitarit kiya jaataa he
 Under this, the central government allocates food grains to the states and union territories for APL and BPL and Antyodaya Anna Yojana
 saarvajanik vitaran pranali ke sanchalay ke liye kendra or rajya sarkaron kii sanyukt jimmedaari hoti he
 While the central government looks after the responsibility of buying, storing, transporting it from one place to another and allocating it in bulk, the state government has the responsibility of distributing it to consumers through fair price shops
 ucchtam nyaayalay ko saunpi gai apni antim report main nyaayamurti vadhwa samiti ne uchit dar dukaanon ke maalikon, transporter, naukarshah or netaaon main santh-ganth kaa zikr karte hue kaha he ki uski siforeeshon ko lagu karke hi is par ankush lagaaya ja sakegaa
 The committee has said that the fair price shop is the focal point of corruption where its owners, transporters, bureaucrats and politicians have nexus to cheat the public
 samiti ke anusaar saarvajanik vitaran pranali ke khadyann kii kaala bazaari ke kaaran asal log iske laabh se vanchit ho jate hai
 In such a situation, the government should take over the operation of corrupt fair rate shops
 iske liye aavashyak he ki rajyon main naagarik aapurti nigam kaa gathan ho jo uchit dar dukaanon par saarvajanik vitaran pranali ke tahat swatantra rup se uchit dar dukaan ke str par khadyann vitaran kaa kaam kare
 The Wadhwa Committee has stated in its recommendations that it would be better to run fair price shops rather than those run by private individuals if corporations, panchayati raj institutions, cooperative societies and self-run groups of women run them at the state level
 samiti ne kaha he, ‘‘korporation ke sanchaalan main hone vaale kisi bhi nuksaan kii bharpai ke liye sarkaar ke bajet main praavdhaan hona chahie
 Where there are no shops and godowns for fair price shops, the government and corporation should build them on the lines of Mother Dairy or ATM or Post Office
 is tarah ke nigam kii kaman bhartiya prashasnic seva ke adhikari ko di jaani chahie
 '' vadhwa samiti ne kaha ki garibi kii rekha se upar jivan yaapan karne vaale pariwaron kii shrenee khatm kii jaani chahie kyonki yah khadyann kaala bazaar main bhejne kaa ek bada jariya he
 The committee has said that if the court feels that it is not possible to abolish this category, then the scope of this category can be considered to be limited to families with annual income of one lakh rupees
 samiti ke anusaar pradhan mantri se lekar nichle str par sabhi saarvajanik vitaran pranali ko durust karne or ise punargathit karne kii himaayat kar chuke hai
 The revival of this system requires drastic steps
 tippaniyan The report said that more than five lakh fair rate shops in the country distribute food grains under the public distribution system
 iske tahat hi kendra sarkaar apiel or bipiel or antyoday ann yojana ke liye rajyon or kendra shasit pradeshon ko khadyann aavantit karti he
 Central and state governments have joint responsibility for the operation of the public distribution system
